				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Alles nur nach Gottes Willen, BWV 72 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>6 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1726
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Sacred_cantatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Sacred cantatas</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Cantatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Cantatas</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Religious_works&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Religious works</a></span>; <span class="expandline" title="34 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_3_voices%2C_mixed_chorus%2C_orchestra&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For 3 voices, mixed chorus, orchestra</a></span>; <h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<h4> <span class="mw-headline" id="Commentary_on_the_movements">Commentary on the movements</span></h4>
<ol><li>Chorus: Alles nur nach Gottes Willen. A movement propelled by the sixteenth notes in the violins. Bach here replaces an aria (proscribed by the librettist) with a chorus. 
</li><li>Recitativo (Alto): O selger Christ, der allzeit seinen Willen. Secco recitative-arioso. 
</li><li>Aria (Alto): Mit allem, was ich hab und bin. The alto starts off immediately here; violins are the obbligato. After the introductory words, we then hear the instrumental ritornello. 
</li><li>Recitativo (Bass): So glaube nun! Secco recitative. 
</li><li>Aria (Soprano): Mein Jesus will es tun, er will dein Kreuz versÃ¼Ãen. Oboe and strings serve as accompaniment. 
</li><li>Choral: Was mein Gott will, das g'scheh allzeit. A plain chorale setting. 
</li></ol>
